<script>
    var depositResultPopup = true;
    var depositResultMethod = '';

    $(".depositModalLazyLoadPre").on('hidden.bs.modal', function () {
        $(this).remove()
    });


    $('#depositingModal').on('shown.bs.modal', function (e) {
        openLazyLoadDepositModal();
    })

    function depositModal() {
        if (isUserLoggedIn) $('#depositingModal').modal('show')
        else $('.depositModalLazyLoadPre').modal('show')
        sideMenu.closeMenu();
    }

    function cleanUrl() {
        var clean_uri = location.protocol + "//" + location.host + location.pathname;
        window.history.replaceState({}, document.title, clean_uri);
    }

    function depositNotice(messageType, title, message) {

        let body = '<div class="deposit-result-message-heading">' + message + '</div><br>';

        if (messageType.toLowerCase() != 'success' && messageType.toLowerCase() != 'info') {
            body += '<button onclick="openDepositPage();swal.close();" autofocus=false class="swal2-confirm swal2-styled swal2-styled-no-border">Deposit Now</button>&nbsp;';
        }
        body += '<button onclick="swal.close();"  autofocus=false class="swal2-confirm swal2-styled swal2-styled-no-border">Close</button>';

        Swal.fire({
            icon: messageType,
            title: title,
            text: message,
            html: body,
            showCancelButton: false,
            showConfirmButton: false
        })
    }

    // kill it in other processes
    function closeDepositModal() {
        if (isUserLoggedIn) $('#depositingModal').modal('hide')
        else $('.depositModalLazyLoadPre').modal('hide')
    }

    function getUrlParameter(sParam) {
        var sPageURL = window.location.search.substring(1),
            sURLVariables = sPageURL.split('&'),
            sParameterName,
            i;

        for (i = 0; i < sURLVariables.length; i++) {
            sParameterName = sURLVariables[i].split('=');

            if (sParameterName[0] === sParam) {
                return sParameterName[1] === undefined ? true : decodeURIComponent(sParameterName[1]);
            }
        }
    }

    function setDespositResultAndRedirect(result) {
        if (depositResultPopup) {
            if (document.location.pathname != localStorage.getItem('Current_location') && localStorage.getItem('Current_location') != null) {
                if (typeof depositResultPopup !== 'undefined' && depositResultPopup) {
                    $('#mainBody > .body-content:last').html('<h2 style="text-align: center"><div class="loadingGif deposit-result-loading-wheel" align="center" ></div><br><span  data-translate-set="DepositFundsContent" data-translate-key="deposit-result-loading-text" class="deposit-result-loading-text">Loading...</span></h2>');
                }
            }
        }

        if (depositResultMethod == '' || depositResultMethod == 'localstorage') {
            $(document).ready(function () {
                if (typeof depositResultPopup !== 'undefined' && depositResultPopup) {
                    window.setTimeout(function () {
                        localStorage.setItem('depositResult', result)
                        let locationToRedirect = localStorage.getItem('Current_location').replace(/\/\/*/g, "/");
                        if (document.location.pathname != locationToRedirect && locationToRedirect != null && document.location.pathname != localStorage.getItem('Current_location') && localStorage.getItem('Current_location') != null) window.location.href = locationToRedirect;
                    }, 10);
                }
                else if (result == 1) {
                    document.location.href = '/Account/ThankYouDeposit';
                }
            })
        }
        else {
            if (depositResultPopup) {
                if (document.location.pathname != localStorage.getItem('Current_location') && localStorage.getItem('Current_location') != null) window.location.href = localStorage.getItem('Current_location') + '?depositModal=' + result;
            }
        }
    }

    $(function () {

        //load the alerts || the modal itself - but only if it's there
        var modalCheck = $('#depositingModal');

        
            if (modalCheck) {

            let dpStorage = localStorage.getItem('depositResult');
            if (dpStorage == null) dpStorage = '';
            let depositResult = dpStorage != '' ? dpStorage : getUrlParameter('depositModal');

            switch (depositResult) {
                case '1':
                    depositNotice('success', 'Success!', 'Your deposit was successful');
                    gax.BankingDepositResultPageNoMethodSpecifiedNew_EventTracking('Success');
                    Swal.isVisible() ? cleanUrl() : false;
                    break;
                case '3':
                case '4':
                case '5':
                    depositNotice('warning', 'Cancelled', 'You have cancelled your deposit');
                    gax.BankingDepositResultPageNoMethodSpecifiedNew_EventTracking('Cancelled');
                    Swal.isVisible() ? cleanUrl() : false;
                    break;
                case 'error':
                case '8':
                    depositNotice('error', 'Failed', 'Your deposit attempt has failed. Please try again');
                    gax.BankingDepositResultPageNoMethodSpecifiedNew_EventTracking('Failed');
                    Swal.isVisible() ? cleanUrl() : false;
                    break;
                case '9':
                    if (modalCheck) depositNotice('info', 'Pending', 'Your deposit transaction is being verified');
                    gax.BankingDepositResultPageNoMethodSpecifiedNew_EventTracking('Pending');
                    Swal.isVisible() ? cleanUrl() : false;
                    break;
                case 'launch':
                    depositModal();
                    break;
            }

            if (localStorage.getItem('depositResult') != null && localStorage.getItem('depositResult') != '') {
                localStorage.setItem('depositResult', '')
            }

        }
    })

</script>

<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        document.getElementById("accountOptionsModal").appendChild(document.getElementById('modal-dialog-id'));
    });
    if (accountOptionsPopUpEnabled) {
        window.onpageshow = function (event) {
            if (event.persisted) {
                if (sessionStorage.getItem('accountOptionsSelected')) {
                    $('[data-account-option-name="' + sessionStorage.getItem('accountOptionsSelected').toLowerCase() + '"]').prop('selected', true);
                }
            }
        };
    }
    function LoadType(select) {
        var accountOptionUrl = $(select).find(":selected").attr('data-acc-option-url');
        var id = $(select).find(":selected").attr('data-acc-option-id');
        var type = $(select).find(":selected").attr('data-acc-option-type');
        var name = $(select).find(":selected").attr('data-acc-option-name');
        var optionId = $(select).find(":selected").attr('id')

        if (name == 'Deposit Funds') {
            gax.BankingDepositEntryPoint_EventTracking("HamburgerMenu DepositButton");

            (swiftEndEnabled && !swiftEndVerified && !securityFlagForSwiftendEnabled) ? account.showSwiftEndPopup() : depositModal();
        } else {
            if (type == 'href') {
                window.location.href = accountOptionUrl
            }
            else if (type == 'onclick') {
                homePage.ShowAccountOptionsModal(accountOptionUrl, id, name);
                homePage.updateSelect(optionId);
            }
        }
    }

</script>

<script>
                        $(function () {
                            var navBarTop = $('.navbar-customTop').height();
                            var navBar = $('#nav-link-container').height();
                            var activeNav = localStorage.getItem('active-nav');

                            var scrollIn = $('#vertMenu > .active')

                            scrollToActiveNavItem();

                            if ($('.header-container').is(':visible')) {
                                if (document.location.href.toLocaleLowerCase().indexOf('account/paymentresult') == -1) {
                                    $('.header-container').attr('style', 'height:' + (navBarTop + navBar) + 'px !important');
                                }
                            }
                            $('#navbar_more').removeAttr('onclick');

                            $('#navbar_more').on('click', function (event) {
                                $(this).parents().find('#vertMenu').toggleClass('expand')
                                $('#overlay1').toggle()

                                if ($('#vertMenu').hasClass('expand')) {
                                    $('#navbar_more').find('i').removeClass('fa-chevron-down').addClass('fa-chevron-up')
                                    $('#navbar_more').find('span').text('Less')
                                    $('body').addClass('lock')
                                } else {
                                    $('#navbar_more').find('i').removeClass('fa-chevron-up').addClass('fa-chevron-down')
                                    $('#navbar_more').find('span').text('More')
                                    $('body').removeClass('lock')
                                    scrollToActiveNavItem()
                                }

                                $('#overlay1').on('click', function () {
                                    if ($('#vertMenu') && $('#vertMenu').hasClass('expand')) {
                                        $('#vertMenu').toggleClass('expand')
                                        $('#overlay1').toggle()

                                        $('#navbar_more').find('i').removeClass('fa-chevron-up').addClass('fa-chevron-down')
                                        $('#navbar_more').find('span').text('More')
                                        $('body').removeClass('lock')
                                        scrollToActiveNavItem()
                                    }
                                })
                            })
                        })

                        function scrollToActiveNavItem() {
                            setTimeout(function () {
                                var active = $(".nav-link-item.active");
                                if (active != null && active[0] != null) {
                                    var left = active.position().left;
                                    var currScroll = $("#vertMenu").scrollLeft();
                                    var contWidth = $('#vertMenu').width() / 2;
                                    var activeOuterWidth = active.outerWidth() / 2;
                                    left = left + currScroll - contWidth + activeOuterWidth - 30;

                                    $('#vertMenu').animate({
                                        scrollLeft: left
                                    }, 500);
                                }
                            }, 200);
                        }
                    </script>

    <style>
        @media screen and (max-width: 768px) {
            .market-grouping .mg-tab-container .mg-tabs {
                overflow: visible;
                display: inline-block;
                width: 100%;
                max-width: calc(100% - 227px) !important;

                width: 100% !important;

<script>
    function getMarketTypeDict(_eventId, _FeedDataTypeId) {
        var currentEventId = localStorage.getItem("_eventId");
        // If not populated yet or if the event id has changed then we do call
        if ((marketGrouping.listAllMarketTypes == null || marketGrouping.listAllMarketTypes.length <= 0)
            || (typeof (currentEventId) != 'undefined' && currentEventId != _eventId)) {
            pat.get("/Bet/EventMultiMarketTypes", {
                'eventId': _eventId, 'FeedDataTypeId': _FeedDataTypeId
            }).done(function (resp) {
                if (resp != null) {
                    marketGrouping.listAllMarketTypes = resp.Data;
                    localStorage.setItem("_eventId", _eventId);
                    // console.log(resp.Data);
                }
            });
        }
        homePage.closeOverlay();
    }
    //Scroll to top of All tab when AllMarkets button is clicked
    $("#AllMarketsButton").on("click", function () {
        $(document).scrollTop(0);
    });
    function switchTab(id, isDropItem) {
        homePage.showOverlay();
        var _eventId = $('#multimarketTabPages').parent().attr('id');
        var _FeedDataTypeId = $("#" + _eventId).attr('data-markettypecategory');
        var _loadedAllMarkets = localStorage.getItem("loadedAllMarkets");
        var _isLastLazyLoaded = localStorage.getItem("lastIsLazyLoaded");
        var _doLoadAllForSearch = localStorage.getItem("doLoadAllForSearch");
        // Determine if we need to load all
        var loadAll = false;
        if ((id !== "00000000-0000-0000-da7a-000000710001" &&
            id !== "00000000-0000-0000-da7a-000000710002" &&
            id !== "00000000-0000-0000-da7a-000000710003" &&
            id !== "00000000-0000-0000-da7a-000000710099") || (_doLoadAllForSearch != null && _doLoadAllForSearch == "true")) {
            loadAll = true;
        } else if ((id === "00000000-0000-0000-da7a-000000710001" || id === "00000000-0000-0000-da7a-000000710099")
            && (_doLoadAllForSearch != null && _doLoadAllForSearch == "true")) {
            loadAll = true;
        } else if (id === "00000000-0000-0000-da7a-000000710003" || (_doLoadAllForSearch != null && _doLoadAllForSearch == "true")) { // We also load all on build a bet but filter out the visibility
            loadAll = true;
            $('.tips-mobile-container').addClass("hidden");
            $('.mg-betooster-toggle').addClass("betBoosterBulbOff");
            $('.mg-betooster-toggle').addClass("toggle-clicked");
            $('#toggle-betbooster-widget').addClass("icon-clicked");
        }
        if (id != "00000000-0000-0000-da7a-000000710003") {
            $('.mg-betooster-toggle').removeClass("betBoosterBulbOff"); 
        }
        if ($("#multimarketTabPages").attr('data-initial-load') == "True" ||
            ((typeof (_loadedAllMarkets) == "undefined" || _loadedAllMarkets == null || _loadedAllMarkets == "false") &&
                (_isLastLazyLoaded == null || typeof (_isLastLazyLoaded) == "undefined") && loadAll == true)) {
            localStorage.removeItem('_eventId');
            localStorage.removeItem("lastIsLazyLoaded");
            localStorage.removeItem("doLoadAllForSearch");
            localStorage.removeItem(id + 'accordPageNum');
            localStorage.removeItem("loadedAllMarkets");
            localStorage.setItem("emptyGroup", document.getElementById("empty-group").outerHTML);
            if (loadAll == true) {
                localStorage.setItem("loadedAllMarkets", true);
                localStorage.setItem("lastIsLazyLoaded", true);
            } else {
                localStorage.setItem("loadedAllMarkets", false);
            }

            var paramData = { 'eventId': _eventId, 'FeedDataTypeId': _FeedDataTypeId, 'isPopular': false, 'pageNum': 1, 'isFullView': false, 'loadAll': loadAll };

            if (loadEventMultiMarketViaAjax) {
                paramData["brandId"] = BrandId;
                paramData["language"] = currentLanguage;
            }
            var _url = (loadEventMultiMarketViaAjax ? "/Ajax/GetEventMultiMarket" : "/Bet/EventMultiMarket");
            pat.get(_url, paramData)
                .done(function (data) {
                    handleMultiEventData(data, _eventId, _FeedDataTypeId, loadAll, id);
                });
        } else {
            marketGrouping.FilterTabs(id, 10);
            setTimeout(function () {
                homePage.closeOverlay();
            }, 500);
            if (fasearch)
                $("#mtSearch").focus();
            if (id == "00000000-0000-0000-da7a-000000710099") {
                marketGrouping.showOnlyFavorites();
            }
        }
        // HIDE LOAD FOR BUILD A BET
        if (id === "00000000-0000-0000-da7a-000000710003") {
            $("#loadMore").hide();
        }
        // SHOW LOAD ALL MARKETS FOR POPULAR
        if (id === "00000000-0000-0000-da7a-000000710002") {
            $("#AllMarkets").show(); }
        else {
            $("#AllMarkets").hide(); }
        // LOAD MORE START
        _loadedAllMarkets = localStorage.getItem("loadedAllMarkets"); // refresh
        _isLastLazyLoaded = localStorage.getItem("lastIsLazyLoaded"); // refresh
        if (id === "00000000-0000-0000-da7a-000000710001" &&
            (typeof (_loadedAllMarkets) == "undefined" || _loadedAllMarkets == null || _loadedAllMarkets == "false")) {
            $("#loadMore").show();
            $("#loadMoreButton").click(function () {
                $("#loadMore").hide();
                $("#loader").show();
                // Call next page batch we already loaded page 1 here
                var currentPage = parseInt(localStorage.getItem(id + 'accordPageNum'));
                if (isNaN(currentPage) || typeof (currentPage) == 'undefined' || currentPage == null) {
                    currentPage = 2;
                    localStorage.setItem(id + 'accordPageNum', currentPage);
                    marketGrouping.retrieveEventMarketGroupsForUpdate(currentPage);
                } else if (typeof (currentPage) != 'undefined' && currentPage > 1) {
                    marketGrouping.retrieveEventMarketGroupsForUpdate(currentPage);
                } else {
                    // Call page update
                    marketGrouping.invokePageUpdate();
                    $("#loader").hide();
                    $("#loadMore").show();
                }
                if (id == "00000000-0000-0000-da7a-000000710099") {
                    marketGrouping.showOnlyFavorites();
                }
            });
        }
        // LOAD MORE END
        //for All Markets button if user is on Mobile
        if (id === "00000000-0000-0000-da7a-000000710001" && isDropItem == false && window.innerWidth <= 768) {
            isDropItem = true;
        }
        //WIP-BELOW
        if (isDropItem) {
            $('#selectButton > span').text($('#' + id).text());
            $('#selectButton').addClass('selected');
            $('#extra-groups li').removeClass('selected');
            $('#' + id).addClass('selected');
            $('#extra-groups').hide();
            $('#selectButton').removeClass('open');
            $('#selectButton').attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
        } else {
            $('#selectButton > span').text();
            $('#selectButton').removeClass('selected');
        }
        $(".mg-tab span").removeClass('selected');
        $(".mg-dropdown span").first().addClass('selected');
        $("#" + id + " span").first().addClass('selected');
        var currentToggle = '#multimarketTabPages #_AllOutcomes .accordionArrows';
        var fisrtChild = $("#multimarketTabPages").find("#_AllOutcomes").find(".container-panel").first()
            .find(".acc-header123");
        fisrtChild.css('height', 'auto');
        var toggleCounter = 0;
        $(currentToggle).each(function (i) {
            toggleCounter++;
            if (toggleCounter <= 5) {
                if (!$(this).hasClass('fa-angle-up')) {
                    $(this).removeClass('fa-angle-down');
                    $(this).addClass('fa-angle-up');
                }
            }
        });


        //if ($("#multimarketTabPages").attr('data-initial-load') == "False") {
        //    homePage.closeOverlay();
        //}
        if (id == "00000000-0000-0000-da7a-000000710099") {
            marketGrouping.showOnlyFavorites();
        }
    }

    function handleMultiEventData(data, eventId, feedDataType, loadAll, tabId = null) {
        if (loadAll == true) {
            $("#_AllOutcomes .container-panel").html(data);
            $("#_AllOutcomes .container-panel").append(localStorage.getItem("emptyGroup"));
        } else {
            $("#_AllOutcomes .container-panel").append(data);
        }
        if (data == null || $("div", data).length <= 20) {
            $("#loaderText").html("End of results");
            $("#loader").fadeOut(850);
            $("#loadMore").hide();
            localStorage.setItem("loadedAllMarkets", true);
            localStorage.setItem("lastIsLazyLoaded", true);
        }

        if (tabId !== null) {
            marketGrouping.FilterTabs(tabId);
            // Apply lazy load
            localStorage.setItem("accordionTabID", tabId.toString());
            if (tabId == "00000000-0000-0000-da7a-000000710099") {
                marketGrouping.showOnlyFavorites();
            }
        }

        marketGrouping.handleSBVgrouping();
        $("#multimarketTabPages").attr('data-initial-load', 'False');
        if (fasearch) {
            $("#mtSearch").focus();
        }
        // Add data to current list
        marketGrouping.addToCurrentMarketTypeDictionary(eventId, $('#_AllOutcomes .search-link'));
        marketGrouping.removeDuplicateMarkets();
        // marketGrouping.ApplyLazyLoad(); // TODO: To enable lazy load scroll load (comment this out)
        // Get market type dictionary for all
        getMarketTypeDict(eventId, feedDataType);
        
        setTimeout(function () {
            homePage.closeOverlay();
        }, 500);
    }

    $(document).ready(function () {
        var loc = window.location.pathname.toLowerCase();
        if (loc.toLowerCase() === "/event/inplay" ||
            loc.toLowerCase() === "/event/livesport" ||
            (loc.toLowerCase() === "/bet/eventmultimarket" && $('#multi-head').hasClass('inPlayBg'))) {
            $(".header-btn a").attr('href', '/Event/LiveSport');
        }
        if (global.getCookie("Stats") == "Yes-Please") {
            $('.lmt-container-new, .lmt-container-old').removeClass('hidden');
            $('.mg-stats-toggle').removeClass("toggle-clicked");
            $('#toggle-stats').removeClass("icon-clicked");
            loadStatsInfo();
        }
        var selectedPageNoCookie = global.getCookie('selectedSportPageNo');
        if (selectedPageNoCookie !== undefined && selectedPageNoCookie !== "") {
            eventDisplay.createIsBackCookie("true");
        }
        $('#betslip-list').find('li').each(function () {
            var outcomeId = $(this).attr('id');
            outcomeId = outcomeId.substr(outcomeId.indexOf('-') + 1);
            var outcomeDisabledElement = $(".inplay.disableElement[id='" + outcomeId + "']");
            if (outcomeDisabledElement) {
                $(outcomeDisabledElement).addClass('disableSelectedElement').removeClass('disableElement');
            }
        });
        homePage.closeOverlay();
    });
    $("#exp-search").on('click', function () {
        $("#loadMore").hide();
        fasearch = true;
        localStorage.setItem("doLoadAllForSearch", true);
        $("#00000000-0000-0000-da7a-000000710001").trigger('click');
        $(".mg-search").toggleClass("search-expanded");
        $(this).toggleClass("search-icon-expanded");
        $(this).toggleClass("md-toggle-search md-toggle-times");
        if (!$(this).hasClass('md-toggle-times')) {
            $("#mtSearch").focusout();
            $("#mtSearch").val('');
            $("#mtSearch").trigger('keyup');
            fasearch = false;
        } else {
            $('.md-toggle-times').on('click',
                function () {
                    $("#mtSearch").blur();
                })
        }
        $(".mg-tabs").toggleClass("left-indent");
        marketGrouping.closeDd();
    });
    $("#toggle-stats").on('click',
        function () {
            if (global.getCookie("Stats") == "Yes-Please") {
                global.eraseCookie("Stats");
            } else {
                global.setCookie("Stats", "Yes-Please");
            }
            $(".mg-stats-toggle").toggleClass("toggle-clicked");
            $(this).toggleClass("icon-clicked");
            $('.player-main').addClass('hidden');
            $('#liveplayer').addClass('hidden');
            $('#liveplayerMobile').addClass('hidden');
            $('.player-main').addClass('media-hidden');
            $('#liveplayer').addClass('media-hidden');
            $('#liveplayerMobile').addClass('media-hidden');

    // TODO: Implement search logic to accomodate lazy loading with paging.
    $('#mtSearch').keyup(function () {
        if (searchTimeout != null || typeof (searchTimeout) != 'undefined') {
            clearTimeout(searchTimeout);
        }
        var txt = $('#mtSearch').val();
        if (txt.length <= 2) {
            if (txt.length <= 0) { // Reload to original
                homePage.showOverlay();
                $("#_AllOutcomes .container-panel .search-link").show();
                marketGrouping.FilterTabs("00000000-0000-0000-da7a-000000710001");
                // Re-bind
                // $(window).bind("scroll", marketGrouping.scrollBind); // TODO: To enable lazy load scroll load (comment this out)
                var _isLastLazyLoaded = localStorage.getItem("lastIsLazyLoaded");
                if (_isLastLazyLoaded == null || typeof (_isLastLazyLoaded) == "undefined") {
                    $("#loadMore").show();
                } else if (_isLastLazyLoaded == "true") {
                    $("#loadMore").hide();
                }
                homePage.closeOverlay();
            }
            return;
        }
        $("#loadMore").hide();
        // Slow it down
        searchTimeout = setTimeout(function () {
            // homePage.showOverlay();
            $("#accordNavButtons").hide();
            $('.search-link').hide();
            // marketGrouping.searchMarkets(txt); // Invoke search // TODO: Comment this out for server compare search
            $('.search-link').each(function () {
                if ($(this).attr("data-marketTitle").toUpperCase().indexOf(txt.toUpperCase()) != -1) {
                    $(this).show();
                } else {
                    $(this).hide();
                }
            });
            if ($('#mtSearch').val()) {
                $("#searchclear").show();
            } else {
                $("#searchclear").hide();
            }
        }, 1500);
    });
    $("#searchclear").on('click',
        function () {
            var _isLastLazyLoaded = localStorage.getItem("lastIsLazyLoaded");
            if (_isLastLazyLoaded == null || typeof (_isLastLazyLoaded) == "undefined") {
                $("#loadMore").show();
            } else if (_isLastLazyLoaded == "true") {
                $("#loadMore").hide();
            }
            $("#mtSearch").val('');
            $("#searchclear").hide();
            $('.search-link').show();
        });
    function loadStatsInfo() {
        var lmtContainerStats = $('.lmt-container-new.sr-widget');
        if ($('.lmt-container-new').is(":visible") && lmtContainerStats == undefined || lmtContainerStats.length < 1) {
            var widgetLoad = true ? "widgets.lmts" : "widgets.matchhead2head";
            homePage.showStats(52520185, true, false);
        }
    }

    function showModalOverlay() {
        $("#eventAndLeagueModalContent").html("");
        document.getElementById("eventLeagueOverlay").style.display = "block";
    }

        document.getElementById("eventLeagueOverlay").style.display = "none";
    }
    var sportIdConst = '891fe800-d816-e811-80cd-00155d4cf19b';
    var eventIdConst = '032164f9-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';
    function getEventsByLeagueId(leagueId, leagueTitle = "") {
        showModalOverlay();
        var leagueText = document.getElementById("leagueText");
        if (leagueTitle != null && leagueTitle !== '') {
            leagueText.innerText = " / " + leagueTitle;
        }
        document.getElementById("modalRegionBackButton").style.display = "inline";

        pat.get("/Event/GetEventsByLeagueId", { leagueId: leagueId, currentEventId: eventIdConst, sportId: sportIdConst }).done(function (content) {
            $("#eventAndLeagueModalContent").html(content);
            hideModalOverlay();
        });
    }
    function getLeaguesByRegionId(regionId, sportConfigId) {
        showModalOverlay();
        var leagueText = document.getElementById("leagueText");
        document.getElementById("modalRegionBackButton").style.display = "none";       
        leagueText.innerText = "";
        pat.get("/Event/GetLeaguesByRegionId", { regionId: regionId, sportConfigId: sportConfigId }).done(function (content) {
            $("#eventAndLeagueModalContent").html(content);
            hideModalOverlay();
        });
    }

        GetAccountFavorites();

            $('#my-page').addClass('yellow');
        }
    });

function iosAppCheck() {
    function e(e, t) {
        t || (t = window.location.href), e = e.replace(/[\[\]]/g, "\\$&");
        var n = new RegExp("[?&]" + e + "(=([^&#]*)|&|#|$)").exec(t);
        return n ? n[2] ? decodeURIComponent(n[2].replace(/\+/g, " ")) : "" : null
    }
	
    if ("true" === e("isIosApp")) {
		// is ios
		
		function removeIosElements(){
			   var t = document.createElement("style");
				if (t.type = "text/css", window.attachEvent && !window.opera) t.styleSheet.cssText = " .header-container,#mobileBetslipFooter,.seo-wrapper,#seo-wrapper,.navbar {display:none !important};";
				else {
					var n = document.createTextNode(" .header-container,#mobileBetslipFooter,.seo-wrapper,#seo-wrapper,.navbar {display:none !important};");
					t.appendChild(n)
				}
				document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(t);
		};
		
		removeIosElements();

		setTimeout(function(){removeIosElements();}, 1000);


    }
}
iosAppCheck();

<h2>The origins of tennis</h2>
<p>The origins of tennis are hotly contested, but the modern game that we know was popularized in England in the 19th century and is now played in a host countries around the world. In the 18th century, England adopted this sport, leading to the kick-off of the first Wimbledon tournament in 1877.</p>
<p>There are four top tournaments in tennis called the Grand Slam Tournaments and these are often the most competitive and best games to bet on. These are Wimbledon, the US Open, The Australian Open, and the French Open. Millions of people watch these tournaments making tennis a great spectator sport as well. Recently, tennis was added to the Olympics as an official sport.</p>
<p>To summarise the sport itself, tennis is a racket sport that can be played individually against a single opponent (singles) or between two teams of two players each (doubles). Singles is far more popular and the top sportsmen of tennis are often considered massive celebrities. Consider Nadal, Federer, the Williamsâ€™s sisters and greats like Steffi Graf and Pete Sampras.</p>
<p><a href="?register=1">Place your tennis bets</a></p>
<p>The modern form of tennis is maintained by a number of different governing bodies who host tournaments under their own names. The ITF is the (International Tennis Federation) is the governing body of world tennis and is made up of 205 national associations. They are responsible for 3 major national competitions that fans enjoy betting on, the Davis Cup, the Fed Cup and the Hopman Cup.</p>
<p>The other well-known association is the ATP (Association of Tennis Professionals) and it was formed in 1972 with the purpose of protecting the interests of male tennis players. Since 1990, the ATP has been actively involved in organizing the worldwide tennis tour for men. They organize a range of different tournaments at different levels throughout each season and are likely the reason that thereâ€™s always so much tennis to bet on. In contrast to the ATP, the WTA (Womenâ€™s Tennis Association) specifically protects the interests of female players and was formed in 1973.</p>

<script type="text/javascript">
    function expandSEO(el) {
        el.classList.toggle("active");
        var textHolder = el.previousElementSibling;
        if (textHolder.style.maxHeight) {
            textHolder.style.maxHeight = null;
        } else {
            textHolder.style.maxHeight = textHolder.scrollHeight + "px";
        }
    }
</script>

<script>

    $(function() {
        var queryStringMobileNumber = '';
        var queryStringFirstName = '';
        var queryStringLastName = '';
        var queryStringEmail = '';
        var queryStringReferralCode = '';
        var queryStringSignUpCode = '';

        if (queryStringMobileNumber !== "")
            $("#MobileNumber_tmpl").val(queryStringMobileNumber);

        if (queryStringFirstName !== "")
            $("#FirstName_tmpl").val(queryStringFirstName);

        if (queryStringLastName !== "")
            $("#LastName_tmpl").val(queryStringLastName);

        if (queryStringEmail !== "")
            $("#Email_tmpl").val(queryStringEmail);

        if (queryStringReferralCode !== "")
            $("#ReferralCode_tmpl").val(queryStringReferralCode);

        if (queryStringSignUpCode !== "")
            $("#VoucherCode_tmpl").val(queryStringSignUpCode);
    });
    setTimeout(function () { removeParentWithNoChildren(); disableAllCheckboxes() }, 250);
    function disableAllCheckboxes() {
        //SubscriptionToAllCommunicationChildren
        //ReceiveViaAllChannelsChildren
        var subscriptionToAllCommunicationChildren = document.getElementById("SubscriptionToAllCommunicationChildren");
        var receiveViaAllChannelsChildren = document.getElementById("ReceiveViaAllChannelsChildren");
        if (subscriptionToAllCommunicationChildren != undefined && subscriptionToAllCommunicationChildren != null) {
            var subChildren = subscriptionToAllCommunicationChildren.getElementsByTagName("input");
            if (subChildren.length > 0) {
                for (var i = 0; i < subChildren.length; i++) {
                    subChildren[i].disabled = true;
                    subChildren[i].readOnly = true;
                }
            }
        } if (receiveViaAllChannelsChildren != undefined && receiveViaAllChannelsChildren != null) {
            var recChildren = receiveViaAllChannelsChildren.getElementsByTagName("input");
            if (recChildren.length > 0) {
                for (var i = 0; i < recChildren.length; i++) {
                    recChildren[i].disabled = true;
                    recChildren[i].readOnly = true;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    var _offers = [];
    $('input[id^="IsSportWelcomeOfferSelected"]').parent().find('input').each(function () {
        //        $('#ddlWelcomeOffer').append('<option value="' + $(this).val() + '">' + $(this).val() + '</option>');
        _offers.push($(this).val());
    });
    localStorage.setItem('welcomeOffers', JSON.stringify(_offers));
</script>

<script>
    $.validator.addMethod('totalCheck', function (value, element) {
        var isDateValid = isValid($('.DOBDropDownDay').val(), $('.DOBDropDownMonth').val(), $('.DOBDropDownYear').val());
        if (!isDateValid && $("#spanForDOBError").html() == "") {
            document.getElementById('spanForDOBError').classList.remove('hidden');
            $("#spanForDOBError").html("Please enter a valid date of birth.");
            language.translateAtRuntime($("#spanForDOBError"), "ErrorMessages", {
                "data-translate-key": "PleaseEnterAValidDateOfBirth"
            });
        } else if (isDateValid) {
            document.getElementById('spanForDOBError').classList.add('hidden');
            $("#spanForDOBError").html("");
        }

        return isDateValid;
    }, "");

    function daysInMonth(m, y) { // m is 0 indexed: 0-11
        switch (m) {
            case 1:
                return (y % 4 == 0 && y % 100) || y % 400 == 0 ? 29 : 28;
            case 8: case 3: case 5: case 10:
                return 30;
            default:
                return 31
        }
    }

    function isRexDateValid(d, m, y) {
        return m >= 0 && m < 12 && d > 0 && d <= daysInMonth(m, y);
    }

    $(function () {
        $('.DOBDropDown').change(function () {
            if ($('.DOBDropDownDay').val() && $('.DOBDropDownMonth').val() && $('.DOBDropDownYear').val()) {
                var dVal = isValid($('.DOBDropDownDay').val(), $('.DOBDropDownMonth').val(), $('.DOBDropDownYear').val());
                if (!dVal) {
                    if ($("#spanForDOBError").html() == "") {
                        document.getElementById('spanForDOBError').classList.remove('hidden');
                        $("#dob-error").addClass("hidden");
                        $("#spanForDOBError").html("Please enter a valid date of birth.");
                    }
                }
                else {
                    $("#spanForDOBError").html("");
                }
            }
            else {
                $("#spanForDOBError").html("");
            }

            if ($.validator.rules)
                $.validator.rules("remove", "DOBDropDown");
        });
    });

    function daysInMonth(m, y) {
        var ml = parseInt(m);
        var yl = parseInt(y);
        switch (ml) {
            case 2:
                return (yl % 4 == 0 && yl % 100) || yl % 400 == 0 ? 29 : 28;
            case 4: case 6: case 9: case 11:
                return 30;
            default:
                return 31
        }
    }

    function isValid(d, m, y) {
        return y > 1900 && m > 0 && m <= 12 && d > 0 && d <= daysInMonth(m, y);
    }
</script>

<script>

                    var tabArray = [1,2];
                    var largestGroupTemplateId = 2;
                    var maxTabIndex = 2;
                    var minTabIndex = 1;
                    var originalMaxTabIndex = 2;

                    $(tabArray).each(function (i, v) {
                        var tabContainer = $("<div class=\"tab-pane\" id=\"TemplateGroup_" + v + "\"></div>");
                        tabContainer.appendTo("#ze-Tabs");
                        $(".section-" + v).detach().appendTo(tabContainer);
                    });

                    $("#TemplateGroup_" + tabArray[0]).addClass("active");
                    $("#TabHeader_" + tabArray[0]).addClass("active");

                for (var i =0 ; i< tabArray.length; i++)
                {
                 $(`#TabHeader_${tabArray[i]}`).click(function (e) {
                 $("#bckBtn,#nxtBtn").show();
                 $("#step1-header").show();
                 $("#step2-header").hide();

                if ($('.tab-pane.active')[0].id ===  `TemplateGroup_${maxTabIndex}`){
                    $("#regBtn,#regCaptchaDiv").show();
                    $("#nxtBtn").hide();

                }else if ($('.tab-pane.active')[0].id ===  `TemplateGroup_${minTabIndex}`){
                 $("#regBtn,#regCaptchaDiv").hide();
                 $("#bckBtn").hide();

                 }});}

                    $("#nxtBtn").click(function (e) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        var currentTabId =  $('.tab-pane.active')[0].id;



                        if (ValidatePage(currentTabId)) {
                            if (otpRegistrationNigeriaEnabled && !captchaValid) {
                                $("#recaptchaError").toggleClass("hidden", captchaValid); return;
                            }

                          if (otpRegistrationNigeriaEnabled) { account.requestOtpForReg(true); }
                          if ($('.tab-pane.active')[0].id ===  `TemplateGroup_${maxTabIndex-1}`)
                                                    {
                            $('.nav-pills > .active').next('li').find('a').trigger('click');
                            $("#regBtn,#bckBtn,#regCaptchaDiv").removeClass("hidden").show();
                            $("#nxtBtn").hide();
                            $("#step1-header").hide();
                            $("#step2-header").show();
                        }else{
                           $('.nav-pills > .active').next('li').find('a').trigger('click');
                           $("#regBtn,#regCaptchaDiv").removeClass("hidden").hide();
                           $("#bckBtn").removeClass("hidden");
                           $(`#step${currentTabId}-header,#nxtBtn,#bckBtn`).show();
                           if (currentTabId !== 1){
                               $(`#step${currentTabId - 1}-header`).hide();
                                }
                              }
                        }
                        IDTypeChanged($('#IDType_tmpl'));
                        $('#displayOnlyId').val($('#IDNumber_tmpl').val());
                        return false;
                    });

                    $("#bckBtn").click(function (e) {
                       /* e.preventDefault();*/
                        var currentTabId =  $('.tab-pane.active')[0].id;
                        var currentTabDivId = `TemplateGroup_${currentTabId}`;

                        $('.nav-pills > .active').prev('li').find('a').trigger('click');
                        $("#regBtn,#regCaptchaDiv").removeClass("hidden").hide();
                        $("#step1-header,#nxtBtn").show();
                        $("#step2-header").hide();

                        if ($('.tab-pane.active')[0].id === `TemplateGroup_${minTabIndex}`)
                        {
                          $("#bckBtn").addClass("hidden").hide();
                        }
                       IDTypeChanged($('#IDType_tmpl'));

                       return false;

                    });


                    $("#TabHeader_2").click(function (e) {
                        $("#regBtn,#bckBtn,#regCaptchaDiv").removeClass("hidden").show();
                        $("#nxtBtn").hide();
                        $("#step1-header").hide();
                        $("#step2-header").show();
                    });

                    $("#TabHeader_1").click(function (e) {
                        $("#regBtn,#bckBtn,#regCaptchaDiv").hide();
                        $("#nxtBtn").show();
                        $("#step1-header").show();
                        $("#step2-header").hide();
                    });

                    $("#regBtn").click(function (e) {
                        $.validator.addClassRules({
                            DOBDropDown: {
                                totalCheck: true
                            }
                        });

                        let templateGroupToValidateOnReg = 'TemplateGroup_2';

                        if (enableCPBNameMultiStepRegistration){
                         templateGroupToValidateOnReg = $('.tab-pane.active')[0].id;
                        }

                        if (ValidatePage(templateGroupToValidateOnReg) && captchaValid) {
                            homePage.showOverlay();
                            clonedIdTypeDisplay = null;
                            clonedIdDisplay = null;
                            hasRegisterButtonBeenPressed = true;
                        } else {
                            $(".DOBDropDown").rules("remove", "totalCheck");
                            $("#recaptchaError").toggleClass("hidden", captchaValid);
                            e.preventDefault();
                            return false;
                        }
                    });

                    function ValidatePage(pageId) {
                        let isValid = true;
                          $('#' + pageId + ' :input').each(function () {
                                 let isElementValid = $(this).valid();
                                 if (!isElementValid){
                                     isValid = false;
                                 }
                          });
                        return isValid;
                    }

                    function FinalInputValidation() {
                        if (EmailValidator.validateEmail())
                            return true;
                        return false;
                    }

                    //Always check teh first page of registration
                    $(document).ready(function () {
                       if (!enableCPBNameMultiStepRegistration) {
                           $('#regPills a:first').tab('show');
                        } else {
                              if (isMultiNameSelectCallSuccessfull || hasRegisterButtonBeenPressed )
                                  {
                                      var smallestTemplateGroupWithError = GetSmallestTemplateGroupWithError();

                                      if (smallestTemplateGroupWithError !== 100){
                                           $(`#TabHeader_${smallestTemplateGroupWithError}`).find('a').trigger('click');
                                        if (smallestTemplateGroupWithError === maxTabIndex){
                                                             $("#regBtn,#regCaptchaDiv,#bckBtn").removeClass('hidden').show();
                                                             $("#nxtBtn").hide();

                                                          }else if (smallestTemplateGroupWithError === minTabIndex){
                                                           $("#regBtn,#regCaptchaDiv,#bckBtn").hide();
                                                           $("nxtBtn").removeClass('hidden').show();

                                                           }

                                      }
                                  }
                           }
                    });

                    var templateSectionIdsToExclude = [];

                    if (enableCPBNameMultiStepRegistration && (!isMultiNameSelectCallSuccessfull || ($('#IDType_tmpl').val() === "Passport") && !hasRegisterButtonBeenPressed)){
                        for (let i = 0; i < tabArray.length; i++){
                           if (tabArray[i] === 1){
                               continue;
                           }
                           console.error(`Adding Exclude: #TemplateGroup_ + ${tabArray[i]}`);
                            templateSectionIdsToExclude.push(tabArray[i]);
                        }
                    }

                           console.error(`Exclude Array: ${templateSectionIdsToExclude} success: ${isMultiNameSelectCallSuccessfull} isPassport: ${ $('#IDType_tmpl').val()}`);

                    if ('False' === 'False' && isSignUpTemplatesVisible(tabArray, templateSectionIdsToExclude)){
                       let smallestTabGroupWithError = GetSmallestTemplateGroupWithError();
                        $(`#TabHeader_${smallestTabGroupWithError}`).find('a').trigger('click');
                        console.error(`show error ${smallestTabGroupWithError}`);
                        location.href = `#TemplateGroup_${smallestTabGroupWithError}`;
                        history.replaceState(null,null,location.href);
                    }

<script>
        function UpdateBetCounter() {
            if (window.loginObject != null) {
                $(".betslipCountBadgeCount").text(window.loginObject.betCount);
                if (window.loginObject.isLoggedIn === "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000") {
                    $("#NotLoggedInPartial").show();
                } else {
                    $("#LoggedInPartial").show();
                    $('#depositMethodsNGbtn').hide();
                    //Update the account values
                    $("#messageCountBadge").text(window.loginObject.inboxCount);

                    if (!enableStaggeredBalanceRender) {
                        $("#cashAmount").text(ToThousandSeparator((Math.floor(window.loginObject.cashBalance * 100) / 100)));
                        $("#freebetBtn").text("Free Bet: " + ToThousandSeparator(window.loginObject.freeBetBalance));
                        if ($(".balance-label").length) {
                            $('.balance-label-amount, .mobile-cash').text(currency + ToThousandSeparator(window.loginObject.cashBalance));
                        }
                        if (enableStaggeredBalanceRender == false) {
                            account.updateBalanceProgress();
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    </script>

                    document.location.href = '/?depositModal=launch'
                }
            }
            else {
                document.location.href = '/?depositModal=launch'
            }
        }
        else {
            document.location.href = '/Account/MyAccount';
        }
    }
